  "new_string": "  private checkPlantUMLAvailability(): void {\n    try {\n      const { spawnSync, execSync } = require('child_process');\n      // Try spawnSync first, then fall back to which + execSync\n      const result = spawnSync('plantuml', ['-version'], { timeout: 15000 });\n      if (result.status === 0) {\n        this.plantumlAvailable = true;\n        log(`PlantUML availability: true (spawnSync)`, 'info');\n        return;\n      }\n      // spawnSync may fail in subprocess contexts — try which + exec as fallback\n      try {\n        execSync('which plantuml', { timeout: 5000 });\n        this.plantumlAvailable = true;\n        log(`PlantUML availability: true (which fallback)`, 'info');\n        return;\n      } catch {\n        // which failed too\n      }\n      this.plantumlAvailable = false;\n      process.stderr.write(`[InsightGen] PlantUML check failed: status=${result.status} signal=${result.signal} error=${result.error}\\n`);\n      log(`PlantUML availability: false (status=${result.status}, signal=${result.signal})`, 'warning');\n    } catch (error) {\n      this.plantumlAvailable = false;\n      log('PlantUML not available - diagram generation disabled', 'warning', error);\n    }\n  }"
}

  "new_string": "  private checkPlantUMLAvailability(): void {\n    try {\n      const { spawnSync, execSync } = require('child_process');\n      // Try spawnSync first, then fall back to which + execSync\n      const result = spawnSync('plantuml', ['-version'], { timeout: 15000 });\n      if (result.status === 0) {\n        this.plantumlAvailable = true;\n        log(`PlantUML availability: true (spawnSync)`, 'info');\n        return;\n      }\n      // spawnSync may fail in subprocess contexts — try which + exec as fallback\n      try {\n        execSync('which plantuml', { timeout: 5000 });\n        this.plantumlAvailable = true;\n        log(`PlantUML availability: true (which fallback)`, 'info');\n        return;\n      } catch {\n        // which failed too\n      }\n      this.plantumlAvailable = false;\n      process.stderr.write(`[InsightGen] PlantUML check failed: status=${result.status} signal=${result.signal} error=${result.error}\\n`);\n      log(`PlantUML availability: false (status=${result.status}, signal=${result.signal})`, 'warning');\n    } catch (error) {\n      this.plantumlAvailable = false;\n      log('PlantUML not available - diagram generation disabled', 'warning', error);\n    }\n  }"
